# Never Miss A Goal Again

| Section                                   | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| ----------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                        | Never Miss a Goal Again                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Purpose**                               | Create a powerful accountability system that turns long-term ambitions into concrete daily actions, ensuring consistent progress on your most important goals.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Scope \- What's Covered**               | \- Making consistent progress on long-term professional or personal goals. \- Providing an external system to maintain focus and accountability.- Breaking down large, intimidating projects into manageable daily steps.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Authority \- XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Review the client's calendar and project boards to identify priorities. \- Propose a single, high-impact daily goal for the client's consideration. \- Update the goal tracker with client-reported progress.- Compile and send a weekly progress summary.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Exceptions \- Must Confirm**            | \- The client must always confirm or set their own final goal for the day.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| **Information & Tools Provided**          | \- A shared [Goal Tracker](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/10-FOIDQaClWA1qwKYN3OFTVV-g8nEBdXUcHqAIK0f3Y/edit?usp=sharing) listing the client's 3-5 long-term goals \- Read-only access to the client's work calendar and relevant project boards (e.g., Asana). \- A messaging app (Text, Slack) for the daily check-in.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Approval Thresholds**                   | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**   | \- XP sends a "Daily Goals Check-in" at a pre-agreed time.- XP sends a "Weekly Progress Summary" at the end of each week.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **SOP \- Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Establish Goals:** Conduct a kickoff to document the client's 3-5 major goals in a shared tracker. 2\. **Daily Review:** Before the check-in time, the XP reviews the client's calendar and projects to identify a key task. 3\. **Check-In:** The XP sends the "Daily Goals Check-in" message, including the proposed focus for the day. 4\. **Update Tracker:** After the client responds, the XP updates the goal tracker with their progress and notes. 5\. **Weekly Summary:** At the end of the week, the XP sends the "Weekly Progress Summary" to the client. |
| **Final Result**                          | The client maintains consistent momentum on their most important goals. The daily loop provides the proactive support, structure, and accountability needed to turn big plans into real, measurable progress.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Agreement**                             | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |

#### Worked Example

| Scenario: A client, a founder, is working towards two major Q4 goals: 1\) Launch a new product and 2\) Hire a VP of Sales. They ask their XP to implement the "Never Miss a Goal Again" playbook to ensure they make consistent daily progress.                                                                                                                  |     |
| :--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **Step 1: Establish Goals**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |     |
| **Action:** In a kickoff meeting, the client and XP document the two major goals in a shared Goal Tracker. They agree on an 8:00 AM daily check-in via text.                                                                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| **Step 2 & 3: Daily Review & Check-In**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| **Action 1:** At 7:45 AM, the XP reviews the client's calendar and Asana board. They see a critical task, "Finalize product spec doc," is due this week.                                                                                                                                                                                                         |     |
| **Action 2:** At 8:00 AM, the XP sends the daily check-in message. **Template Used:** **Daily Goals Loop: Sept 9** **Yesterday's Progress:** How did you do on 'Drafting the job description'? **Today's Focus:** Based on Asana, it looks like the \#1 thing to accomplish today is '**Finalize the product spec doc**.' Does that feel right?                  |     |
| **Step 4: Update Tracker**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     |
| **Action:** The client replies to the text, confirming the goal and their progress. The XP updates the shared Goal Tracker with the client's notes.                                                                                                                                                                                                              |     |
| **Step 5: Weekly Summary**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     |
| **Action:** At the end of the week, the XP reviews the tracker and sends the "Weekly Progress Summary".**Template Used:** **Weekly Goals Summary: Week of Sept 8** **Wins This Week:** Finalized the product spec doc; completed the first draft of the VP of Sales job description. **Focus for Next Week:** Begin user testing interviews for the new product. |     |
| **Final Result**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| The client maintains consistent momentum on their most important goals. The daily prompt from the XP provides the structure and accountability needed to break down their large goals into manageable daily actions, ensuring real, measurable progress is made each week..                                                                                      |     |

Alt version for the goals: [https://docs.google.com/document/d/1ydfYm5IFOVXChZRO7KJewzAMiTR6X6lenharZIkpqdM/edit?tab=t.0](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1ydfYm5IFOVXChZRO7KJewzAMiTR6X6lenharZIkpqdM/edit?tab=t.0)

# Run Life Like a Hotel (systemized living)

# Auto Stock

### Never Run Out of Essentials Again

| Section                                   | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| ----------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                        | Never Run Out of Essentials Again                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Purpose**                               | Save 2-3 hours per week and eliminate last-minute store runs by creating a system to automate the ordering of all household essentials.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| **Scope \- What's Covered**               | \- Automating recurring orders (toiletries, cleaning supplies, pet food). \- Weekly grocery shopping, especially when linked to a meal plan. \- Managing subscriptions for any regularly purchased items.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| **Authority \- XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Set up and manage automated deliveries for pre-approved items. \- Place weekly grocery orders that align with the meal plan and budget. \- Adjust order frequencies based on periodic inventory reviews. \- Update all tabs of the "Smartt Essentials & Budget Tracker" after each order.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Exceptions \- Must Confirm**            | \- Adding any new items or brands to the master list. \- Any order that will exceed the pre-defined budget. \- Switching to a new vendor or delivery service.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Information & Tools Provided**          | \- The **"[Smart Essentials & Budget Tracker](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1rhV1XI0iXFNHLUF1HI-ugyuQQF6DPMe3iTyD-be0SrU/edit?usp=sharing)"** (with Essentials, Budget, and Vendor tabs) serves as the single source of truth. \- Access to preferred online retailer accounts (e.g., Amazon, Instacart). \- A secure method for sharing payment credentials (e.g., 1Password).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| **Approval Thresholds**                   | \- Client to define a budget per order (e.g., "Weekly grocery budget: $XXX").                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**   | \- XP sends an "Order Confirmation" notice via chat/text after any order is placed.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **SOP \- Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Establish Protocol:** Conduct a kickoff to create a master list of items, brands, frequencies, and vendors. 2\. **Set Up Automation:** Use the **"Vendor Tracker"** to log in and set up recurring deliveries based on items in the **"Essentials Tracker"**. 3\. **Manage Manual Orders:** Use the **"Essentials Tracker"** as the shopping list for weekly manual orders 4\. **Review & Adjust:** **Update Tracker:** After each purchase, log the expenditure in the **"Budget Tracker"** 5\. **Confirm Orders:** After each order, send the "Order Confirmation" notice to the client. 6\. Periodically review the entire tracker with the client to adjust items, budgets, or vendors. |
| **Final Result**                          | Household essentials are replenished automatically. The client saves time and mental energy, avoids inconvenient last-minute trips to the store, and never worries about running out of their favorite items again.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Agreement**                             | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

#### Worked Example

| Scenario: The client, Anna, wants to automate her household shopping to save time and gain a clear understanding of her weekly and monthly spending on essentials. She and her XP decide to implement the "Never Run Out of Essentials Again" playbook using the 3-tab "Smart Essentials & Budget Tracker."                                                                                                                                                                |     |
| :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **Step 1: The Kickoff Conversation**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     |
| **Action:** Anna and her XP hold a kickoff call to populate the tracker. Essentials Tracker Tab: They list weekly groceries (milk, eggs, chicken, spinach) and monthly supplies (Blue Bottle coffee, Seventh Generation paper towels, Taste of the Wild dog food). Vendor Tracker Tab: Anna provides access details for Instacart and Amazon via a secure password manager. Budget Tracker Tab: They set the budgets: $200/week for groceries and $100/month for supplies. |     |
| **Step 2: System Setup**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |     |
| **Action 1**: The XP uses the **Vendor Tracker** to log into Anna's Amazon account.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |     |
| **Action 2**: Referencing the **Essentials Tracker**, the XP sets up "Subscribe & Save" for the coffee, paper towels, and dog food. The total monthly cost is $85.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |     |
| **Step 3 & 4: First Grocery Order & Tracking**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |     |
| **Action 1**: The XP logs into Instacart to place the weekly grocery order. They use the **Essentials Tracker** tab as the shopping list. The final cart total is **$188.50**.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |     |
| **Action 2:** The XP immediately navigates to the Budget Tracker tab and enters the new expense, which shows that Anna is still within her weekly budget.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |     |
| **Step 5: Confirmation**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |     |
| **Action:** After placing the order and updating the tracker, the XP sends a confirmation to Anna. **Template Used: Order Placed:** Instacart **Items:** Weekly Groceries **Total Cost:** $188.50 **Delivery ETA:** Saturday, September 6, between 10 AM \- 12 PM **Note:** The Budget Tracker has been updated.                                                                                                                                                           |     |
| **Step 6: Ongoing Review**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| **Action**: At the end of the month, the automated Amazon order of $85 is also logged in the **Budget Tracker**. The XP can now provide a high-level summary: "Hi Anna, quick update for September: We stayed under budget for both groceries and supplies. The tracker is fully updated if you'd like to see the details\!"                                                                                                                                               |     |
| **Final Result**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |     |
| Anna‚Äôs home is consistently stocked with all her preferred items, and she has spent zero time on shopping or planning. More importantly, the **Smartt Essentials & Budget Tracker** gives her a real-time, accurate view of her household spending, providing complete control and peace of mind.                                                                                                                                                                          |     |

### Remote Household Manager

| Section                                   | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| ----------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                        | Remote Household Management                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Purpose**                               | Save over an hour each week and reduce the mental load of managing your household by creating a system for an XP to proactively oversee your home's needs.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Scope \- What's Covered**               | \- Automating the restocking of groceries, pantry items, and supplies. \- Proactively identifying and scheduling home maintenance and repairs. \- Coordinating with a trusted in-home contact (e.g., housekeeper, nanny).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Authority \- XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Place grocery and supply orders within the pre-defined budget.- Schedule routine or pre-approved maintenance and repair services. \- Communicate directly with the in-home contact for status updates.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Exceptions \- Must Confirm**            | \- Any single order or service that exceeds the budget. \- Scheduling major, non-routine, or unexpected repairs. \- Hiring a new, non-pre-approved service provider.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Information & Tools Provided**          | \- A group messaging app to connect the XP and the in-home contact. \- Client defines the weekly "scan" requirements (e.g., "send photos of the fridge and pantry every Friday"). \- Access to preferred vendors for groceries and home services.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Approval Thresholds**                   | \- Client to authorize a budget per action (e.g., "Grocery orders under $200").                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**   | \- XP sends a "Weekly Home Summary" to the client after each weekly check-in.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| **SOP \- Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Establish Protocol:** Connect the XP and in-home contact in a group chat and define the weekly "scan" process. 2\. **Receive Updates:** XP receives weekly photos and updates from the in-home contact. 3\. **Analyze & Action:** XP analyzes the updates to create a list of needs (restocking, repairs). 4\. **Execute:** XP places orders and schedules services according to their authority and budget. 5\. **Report to Client:** XP delivers the "Weekly Home Summary," detailing actions taken and flagging future needs. |
| **Final Result**                          | The client's home is managed proactively in the background. Supplies are replenished and issues are addressed before they require the client's attention, giving them peace of mind and freeing up their mental space.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Agreement**                             | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |

#### Worked Example

| Scenario: The client, who travels frequently for work, wants to ensure their home essentials are always stocked and minor maintenance issues are handled proactively. They have a trusted housekeeper, Maria, who visits every Friday.                                                                                                                                                                               |     |
| :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **Step 1: Establish Protocol**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     |
| **Action:** Following the playbook, the XP creates a WhatsApp group chat to connect with the client and Maria, the in-home contact.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |     |
| **Action:** The XP confirms the weekly "scan" process in the chat: "Hi Maria, as discussed with the client, please send photos of the fridge and pantry every Friday morning. Thank you\!"                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |     |
| **Action:** The client authorizes the budget as per the protocol's approval threshold: "XP, you are authorized for grocery orders up to $200".                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     |
| **Step 2 & 3: Receive Updates and Analyze**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| **Action:** Maria sends photos to the WhatsApp group. The pictures show that milk, eggs, and fresh vegetables are running low. She also sends a photo of a burnt-out lightbulb in a high-ceiling fixture.                                                                                                                                                                                                            |     |
| **Action:** The XP analyzes these updates to create a list of needs: a grocery restock and a handyman service for the lightbulb.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| **Step 4: Execute**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |     |
| **Action:** The XP places an Instacart order for the needed groceries, totaling $162, which is within the pre-defined budget.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |     |
| **Action:** The XP contacts the client's pre-approved handyman service to schedule a visit for the following week to replace the lightbulb, as this falls under "routine maintenance".                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |     |
| **Step 5: Report to Client**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |     |
| **Action**: The XP sends the "Weekly Home Summary" to the client via email. **Template Used:** **Home Status Update:** Week of September 8, 2025 **Actions Taken:** Restocked pantry and fridge staples via Instacart ($162). Scheduled the handyman for Tuesday at 10 AM to replace the hallway lightbulb. **Heads-Up:** Noticed the coffee supply is about halfway. Proposing we add it to the order in two weeks. |     |
| **Final Result**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| The home is managed proactively in the background. The client returns from their work trip to a fully stocked kitchen and a scheduled solution for their maintenance issue, all without their direct involvement. This frees up their mental space and saves them from dealing with household chores upon their return.                                                                                              |     |

# Travel Kit

### Automated Travel Booking

| Section                                   | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| ----------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **Protocol Title**                        | Automated Travel Booking                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Purpose**                               | Save 1-5+ hours per trip and eliminate planning hassle by using a centralized profile of all travel preferences.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| **Scope \- What's Covered**               | \- Initial onboarding to create the comprehensive Travel Profile. \- End-to-end booking for all business and personal travel. \- Management of all travel-related loyalty programs and personal details.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Authority \- XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Research flight, hotel, and ground transport options that align with the Travel Profile. \- Propose 1-2 curated itineraries for client review.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Exceptions \- Must Confirm**            | \- The final itinerary before any non-refundable bookings are made. \- Any proposed options that deviate from the Travel Profile (e.g., non-preferred airlines or hotels).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Information & Tools Provided**          | \- A comprehensive [Travel Profile](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1FSfp7CfozMWI7GiwrGvRdhkfK_1TrRQI0NtKU9t-nVg/edit?usp=sharing) (listing all preferences, loyalty numbers, etc.). \- A secure method for sharing payment credentials. \- Client provides destination and dates for each trip request.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Approval Thresholds**                   | \- Client to define a budget per trip (e.g., "Business travel budget: $XXX").                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**   | \- XP sends a "[Proposed Itinerary](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1FSfp7CfozMWI7GiwrGvRdhkfK_1TrRQI0NtKU9t-nVg/edit?usp=sharing)" for client review and approval. \- XP sends a final "Trip Confirmation" and calendar invites once booked.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **SOP \- Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Create Profile:** Conduct a kickoff meeting to create and approve the client's master Travel Profile. 2\. **Receive Request:** Client provides trip destination and dates. 3\. **Research & Propose:** XP researches options based on the profile and sends 1-2 curated itineraries for approval. 4\. **Book & Confirm:** Once the client approves an option, the XP books all travel components. 5\. **Consolidate & Deliver:** XP creates a single trip itinerary, sends the final confirmation, and adds all events to the client's calendar. |
| **Final Result**                          | Travel is booked perfectly to the client's specifications every time. The client simply states their destination and dates, and a complete, personalized itinerary appears on their calendar without them ever having to search for flights or hotels.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Agreement**                             | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |

#### Worked Example

| Scenario: A client, a consultant, needs to book a trip to New York for a three-day client meeting. Their Travel Profile is already on file with their XP, noting a preference for Delta, Marriott hotels, and a total trip budget of $1,500.                                                                                                                               |     |
| :------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **Step 1 & 2: Profile Created & Request Received**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |     |
| **Action:** The client's master Travel Profile is already complete and approved. The client sends a brief request via email: "I need to be in NYC for meetings from October 6-8. Please book travel.".                                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| **Step 3: Research & Propose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |     |
| **Action 1:** The XP researches options that align with the client's profile. They find a suitable Delta flight and a room at the Marriott Marquis that are both within budget.                                                                                                                                                                                            |     |
| **Action 2:** The XP sends the "Proposed Itinerary" to the client for review. Template Used: Options for Your Trip to NYC Option 1: ‚Ä¢ Flight: Delta, nonstop, LGA, aisle seat confirmed. ‚Ä¢ Hotel: Marriott Marquis, King Room, high floor requested. ‚Ä¢ Total Cost: $1,350 Note: This option aligns with all your preferences. Please let me know if you'd like me to book. |     |
| **Step 4: Book & Confirm**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| **Action:** The client replies with "Looks great, please book it." The XP immediately books all travel components using the client's securely stored credentials.                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| **Step 5: Consolidate & Deliver**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| **Action 1:** The XP creates a single trip itinerary document with all confirmation numbers and details. The XP sends the final "Trip Confirmation" email, attaches the itinerary, and adds all relevant events to the client's calendar.                                                                                                                                  |     |
| **Final Result**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |     |
| The client's entire trip was booked to their exact specifications in under 48 hours with minimal effort on their part. They simply stated their destination and dates and received a complete, personalized itinerary on their calendar.                                                                                                                                   |     |

# Multiply Your Impact (scale without strain)

# Make Friends, Gain Influence

### Monthly Salons / Founder Dinners

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| ---------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Monthly Salons / Founder Dinners                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Purpose**                              | Host curated gatherings that deepen relationships and expand your network effortlessly.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Monthly dinner with \~10 guests. \- Venue: client‚Äôs home (private chef/catered) or restaurant.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Curate invite list of 10 new/interesting people. \- Manage invitations, RSVPs, menu, and logistics.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Any guest not aligned with client‚Äôs network goals. \- Event budget \>$2,000.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Client‚Äôs network list \+ preferences. \- Budget and venue options.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Up to $2,000 ‚Üí XP may proceed. \- $2,000‚Äì$5,000 ‚Üí Notify client. \- Above $5,000 ‚Üí Explicit approval.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- XP proposes guest list 3 weeks prior. \- Weekly update until event.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **T-6 Weeks** ‚Üí Draft invite list \+ propose venue/menu. 2\. **T-4 Weeks** ‚Üí Send invites \+ manage RSVPs. 3\. **T-2 Weeks** ‚Üí Confirm chef/restaurant or catering. 4\. **T-3 Days** ‚Üí Finalize seating, print prompts. 5\. **Day-Of** ‚Üí Ensure set-up, host packet ready. 6\. **Post** ‚Üí XP logs attendees \+ prepares thank-you notes. |
| **Final Result**                         | A seamless, curated dinner where the client shows up as host without logistical burden.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Monthly Salons / Founder Dinners                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |

---

#### **Worked Example**

| Scenario: The client, a respected founder, wants to host an intimate, high-value dinner at their home. The goal is to connect a curated group of 10 local founders and 2 strategic investors in a relaxed setting, allowing for deep conversation and relationship-building. The client's primary objective is to be a present and engaged host, leaving all logistical and executional details to their XP.                |     |
| :-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **T-4 Days: Invitations & RSVP Management**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| **Action:** The XP sends out elegant, personalized invitations via Paperless Post to the curated guest list. They then manage all RSVPs and guest communications, providing the client with regular updates.                                                                                                                                                                                                                |     |
| **T-3 Days: Experience Curation & Final Prep**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |     |
| **Action 1:** With the final guest list confirmed, the XP creates a strategic seating chart designed to place guests with complementary interests or potential synergies next to each other. Action: The XP designs and prints high-quality place cards. On the back of each card, a unique conversation prompt is included to spark meaningful dialogue, such as, "What‚Äôs your biggest delegation breakthrough this year?" |     |
| **Action 2:** The XP sends a final confirmation email to all attendees with the address, timing, and a note about the evening's intimate, salon-style format.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |     |
| **Day-Of: On-Site Execution**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |     |
| **Action:** The XP arrives at the client's home an hour early to coordinate with the private chef and oversee the final setup, ensuring the ambiance is perfect. Action: As guests arrive, the XP greets them, checks them in, and gently guides them, ensuring the evening flows seamlessly and introductions are made.                                                                                                    |     |
| **Post-Event: Follow-Up & Data Capture**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |     |
| **Action 1:** The XP compiles a clean, organized list of all attendees, including their contact details and any relevant notes, for the client‚Äôs records. Action: The XP drafts a personalized thank-you email template for the client to send to each guest, solidifying the connections made during the evening.                                                                                                          |     |
| **Action 2:** The XP drafts a personalized thank-you email template for the client to send to each guest, solidifying the connections made during the evening.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |     |
| **Final Result**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |     |
| The client successfully hosted a high-impact networking event without the stress of managing logistics. They were able to focus entirely on their guests, fostering strong relationships in an effortlessly elegant environment. The post-event follow-up, prepared by the XP, ensured the momentum from the evening was maintained.                                                                                        |     |

### Thoughtful Gift Giving

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Thoughtful Gift Giving (Kids \+ Adults)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Purpose**                              | Ensure every birthday, holiday, and milestone is marked with thoughtful, on-time gifts.                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Kids‚Äô birthday parties. \- Friends‚Äô/family holidays, milestones, or surprise gifts.                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Research age-appropriate gifts via sources like NYT ‚ÄúBest Children‚Äôs Gifts.‚Äù \- Order, wrap, and deliver to home at least 2 weeks in advance. \- Maintain master gift tracker.                                                                                                     |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Gifts \>$200. \- Unfamiliar adults (requires client guidance).                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- List of kids‚Äô classmates \+ friends/family birthdays. \- Corporate/personal card in 1Password.                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Up to $200 ‚Üí proceed. \- $200‚Äì$500 ‚Üí notify client. \- Above $500 ‚Üí explicit approval.                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- XP confirms birthday calendar monthly. \- Slack update once gift is ordered \+ ETA.                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step (Kids)**            | 1\. **Upon Invite** ‚Üí XP logs party date. 2\. **Next Day** ‚Üí Prompt client to ask child what their friend likes. 3\. **T-2 Weeks** ‚Üí Order \+ deliver wrapped gift to home. 4\. **Day Before** ‚Üí Slack reminder: ‚Äú‚úÖ Gift ready for Max‚Äôs party.‚Äù 5\. **Post** ‚Üí Log in Gift Tracker. |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step (Adults)**          | 1\. Maintain calendar of birthdays/holidays. 2\. Research thoughtful gifts aligned with interests. 3\. Order \+ deliver (wrapped or digital). 4\. Confirm with client upon delivery. 5\. Track all gifts in master sheet.                                                             |
| **Final Result**                         | Client always shows up with the perfect gift ‚Äî thoughtful, timely, and stress-free.                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |

#### **Worked Example**

| Scenario: The client is a busy parent whose child has been invited to a friend's 8th birthday party. The goal is to handle the entire gift-giving process‚Äîfrom idea to delivery‚Äîproactively, ensuring a thoughtful, age-appropriate gift is purchased, wrapped, and ready for the party on time.                                                                                     |     |
| :----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **February 1: Invitation Received & Intel Gathering**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |     |
| **Action 1**: The client forwards the birthday party invitation for their child's friend, **Max**, to the XP.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |     |
| **Action 2**: The XP immediately adds the party date to the family calendar and sends a simple prompt to the client: _"Got it\! Could you ask your child what Max is interested in these days so we can find the perfect gift?"_                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| **February 3: Research & Recommendation**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |     |
| **Action 1**: The client replies with a one-word answer: _"dinosaurs."_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |     |
| **Action 2**: The XP researches top-rated dinosaur-themed gifts for 8-year-olds, identifying the **‚ÄúSmithsonian Dino Dig Kit‚Äù** ($65), which was noted as a top pick by the NYT.                                                                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| **February 4: Purchase & Logistics**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| **Action:** The XP orders the gift using the client's pre-approved budget and payment method. They select the gift-wrapping option and schedule the delivery for February 10, well ahead of the party.                                                                                                                                                                               |     |
| **February 14: The Final Reminder**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |     |
| **Action:** The day before the party, the XP sends a clear and concise confirmation to the client, closing the loop and eliminating any last-minute stress.                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| **Final Result**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |     |
| The client received a simple, proactive reminder: ‚Äú‚úÖ Dino Kit ready for Max‚Äôs party tomorrow.‚Äù A high-quality, well-researched, and fully wrapped gift was ready to go without the client having to spend any time on the task. The process ensured their child arrived at the party feeling confident and prepared, effortlessly managing the social obligations of a busy family. |     |

| Scenario: The client's close friend has achieved a major career milestone: being promoted to Partner. To honor the occasion, the client is attending a celebratory dinner on March 1st and wants to present a significant, personalized gift. They create a short, curated list of 2-3 ideas, with the top recommendation being a timeless Montblanc pen that can be engraved.                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
| **February 15: Proposal & Explicit Approval**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |     |

| **Action 1:** The XP places the order, coordinating directly with the vendor to ensure the engraving is executed perfectly. They also request premium gift boxing.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |     |

| **Post-Event: Record Keeping**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |     |
