### Team Recognition Ritual

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Team Recognition Ritual                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| **Purpose**                              | Build a culture of appreciation and recognition to strengthen motivation and team performance.                                                                                                                                             |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Weekly/monthly recognition moments. \- Pre-drafted thank-you notes, shout-outs, and milestone recognitions.                                                                                                                             |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Draft 3‚Äì5 recognition notes weekly. \- Suggest individuals/events worthy of public recognition.                                                                                                                                         |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Any recognition involving sensitive/confidential projects.                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Team roster. \- Project tracker. \- Client‚Äôs voice/style guide.                                                                                                                                                                         |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- XP sends draft recognition notes every Friday. \- Client edits/approves in \<10 minutes.                                                                                                                                                |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Weekly** ‚Üí XP reviews team activity \+ identifies wins. 2\. Draft 3‚Äì5 recognition notes/shout-outs. 3\. Client tweaks/approves in 10 min. 4\. Send via Slack/email/team meeting. 5\. XP logs recognitions in tracker for visibility. |
| **Final Result**                         | Team receives consistent, authentic recognition ‚Üí stronger morale \+ 3x higher likelihood of exceeding targets.                                                                                                                            |
| **Supporting Stat**                      | ‚ÄúEmployees who receive regular recognition are 3x more likely to be highly engaged and productive.‚Äù ‚Äì McKinsey & Company                                                                                                                   |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                   |

#### **Worked Example**

| Scenario: The Engineering team just shipped a new internal tool two weeks early.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |     |
| :---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --- |
| **Weekly Review**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |
| **Action 1**: XP checks with recruiting ‚Üí learns Maria is passionate about climbing, speaks Spanish, and wowed interviewers with her customer-centric thinking..                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |     |
| **Action 2:** XP checks project tracker ‚Üí sees Engineering milestone hit early. XP drafts 3 recognition messages: Slack shout-out: ‚ÄúBig thanks to the Eng team for launching the resource tracker 2 weeks early üôå‚Äîalready saving us time daily.‚Äù Personal note to Sarah (tech lead): ‚ÄúSarah, your leadership made the difference‚Äîthank you for guiding the team so smoothly.‚Äù Thank-you email to the full squad. |     |
| **Friday Approval**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |     |
| **Action:** Client posts Slack shout-out at team meeting start. Emails go out same day.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |     |
| **Post-Event**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |     |
| **Action:** XP logs recognitions in tracker: ‚ÄúEng team recognized for early delivery (Feb 2025).‚Äù                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |     |

| Team feels valued for their effort, morale is high, and culture of appreciation reinforced.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |     |

# Sleep Reset

### Night Nanny

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Night Nanny                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Purpose**                              | Allow parents to rest while XP remotely supports children‚Äôs bedtime and night routines.                                                                                                                     |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Remote supervision via Zoom or networked camera. \- Bedtime routine support (reading, calm-down activities). \- Emergency alert system if escalation needed.                                             |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Set up nightly Zoom session. \- Read to child, keep routine on schedule. \- Call via ‚ÄúFreedom Phone‚Äù if escalation is needed.                                                                            |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Any physical in-person care. \- Medical decisions.                                                                                                                                                       |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Freedom Phone setup. \- Child‚Äôs bedtime routine \+ preferences. \- Camera/Zoom access.                                                                                                                   |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Daily check-in at bedtime. \- Slack/phone alert if child cannot be calmed.                                                                                                                               |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. Schedule nightly Zoom session. 2\. Guide child through bedtime routine. 3\. Optional: reading time (child reads aloud). 4\. Monitor via camera. 5\. Call parent via Freedom Phone if escalation needed. |
| **Final Result**                         | Kids go to bed on time; parents sleep without worry.                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                    |

**Worked Example**

- Bedtime: 7:30pm. XP logs on via Zoom at 7:15.
- Child reads 20 minutes from _Charlotte‚Äôs Web_. XP encourages.
- Lights out by 8:20.
- 8:40 fussing ‚Üí XP waits 10 minutes, resolves. No escalation.
- Parent evening is uninterrupted.

### Sleep Score Scheduling Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Sleep Score Scheduling                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Purpose**                              | Optimize daily schedule based on real-time sleep data.                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Daily sync with client‚Äôs sleep tracking app (Oura, Whoop, etc.). \- Adjust meetings, workouts, and deep work blocks.                                                                                             |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Reschedule non-essential meetings if sleep score is low. \- Prioritize deep work/workouts if score is high.                                                                                                      |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Canceling client-facing external meetings.                                                                                                                                                                       |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Access to sleep app. \- Calendar access. \- List of flexible vs. non-flexible commitments.                                                                                                                       |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Daily 6:30am Slack update with plan adjustments.                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. Sync sleep score at 6:00am. 2\. If low ‚Üí move non-essential meetings, shorten day. 3\. If high ‚Üí add deep work, workout, or stretch goals. 4\. Update calendar by 6:30am. 5\. Notify client with adjusted plan. |
| **Final Result**                         | Client‚Äôs energy is matched to the right work and recovery daily.                                                                                                                                                    |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                            |

#### Worked Sample

6:00 AM: Client's Oura ring reports a low sleep score of 65\.
6:15 AM: XP syncs the data, postpones two non-essential internal meetings to the next day, and blocks a 30-minute recovery period in the afternoon calendar.
6:30 AM: Client receives a Slack update with their adjusted, lighter schedule, allowing them to prioritize recovery without missing critical work.

### Jet Lag Minimizer Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                |
| ---------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Jet Lag Minimizer                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Purpose**                              | Reduce travel fatigue by shifting routines pre- and post-trip.                                                                                                                         |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Adjust bedtime, wake time, meals, and light exposure before/after flights.                                                                                                          |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Create personalized time-shift plan. \- Update calendar with new blocks.                                                                                                            |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Shifts \>2 hours/day.                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Travel schedule. \- Client‚Äôs preferred shift rules (e.g., 30 minutes earlier each night).                                                                                           |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Share Jet Lag Plan 7 days before trip.                                                                                                                                              |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. Receive travel itinerary. 2\. Build time-shift schedule (bed, meals, workouts). 3\. Update client‚Äôs calendar. 4\. Remind daily with adjusted routine. 5\. Post-trip ‚Üí adjust back. |
| **Final Result**                         | Client adapts quickly and avoids major jet lag symptoms.                                                                                                                               |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                               |

**Worked Example**

- Flight: NYC ‚Üí London, March 14\.
- XP plan: Shift bedtime 30 min earlier starting March 10\. Meals adjusted \+ blocked AM light walks in London.
- Calendar updated. Daily reminders sent.
- Result: Client adjusted within 24 hours on arrival.

### Smart Alarm Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                   |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Smart Alarm                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Purpose**                              | Allow XP to remotely set, move, or cancel alarms based on sleep, schedule changes, or cancellations.                                                                      |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Alarm management tied to schedule \+ sleep score.                                                                                                                      |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Set/cancel alarms within agreed hours.                                                                                                                                 |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Canceling alarms for immovable commitments (board calls, flights).                                                                                                     |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Alarm app with XP control. \- Sleep score integration.                                                                                                                 |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                       |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Slack confirmation night before: ‚ÄúAlarm set for 6:30am tomorrow.‚Äù                                                                                                      |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. Review next day‚Äôs calendar at 8pm. 2\. Cross-check with sleep score. 3\. Set alarm accordingly. 4\. Confirm with client. 5\. Adjust if cancellations arise overnight. |
| **Final Result**                         | Client wakes up only when necessary, aligned with energy and schedule.                                                                                                    |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                  |

**Worked Example**

- Sleep Score: 62\. Early 7am call canceled overnight.
- XP adjusts alarm from 6:00 ‚Üí 7:45am.
- Slack message: ‚Äúüîî Adjusted alarm ‚Äî call canceled, catch extra rest. New wake 7:45

### Homework Buddy Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                               |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Homework Buddy                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Purpose**                              | Support child‚Äôs learning by making XP a consistent, patient tutor.                                                                                                                    |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- After-school homework for elementary students. \- Reading, math, projects.                                                                                                         |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Schedule homework block. \- Prepare materials/questions with ChatGPT.                                                                                                              |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Any high-stakes test prep requiring external tutor.                                                                                                                                |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- School curriculum/homework access. \- Child‚Äôs learning preferences.                                                                                                                |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Daily homework sessions (Zoom or in-person if local). \- Weekly progress update to parent.                                                                                         |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. XP receives homework list. 2\. Prepare lesson plan \+ ChatGPT tutor prompts. 3\. Schedule 30‚Äì45 min session. 4\. Work with child patiently. 5\. Share weekly summary with parent. |
| **Final Result**                         | Child develops homework habits and lifelong learning confidence.                                                                                                                      |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                              |

**Worked Example**

- Subject: 4th grade fractions.
- XP sets up Zoom at 4:00pm.
- ChatGPT prompt: ‚ÄúAct as patient 4th grade tutor.‚Äù
- Child completes 90% of problems independently.
- Weekly summary: ‚Äú‚úÖ Fractions much stronger; next week focus on decimals.‚Äù

| **Final Result**                         | Client conserves willpower for strategic choices; daily friction eliminated.                                                                                                  |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                      |

# Money Check

### The Recurring Cost & Subscription Audit

| Section                                   | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| ----------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                        | The Recurring Cost & Subscription Audit                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Purpose**                               | Save hundreds or thousands of dollars per year and declutter finances by identifying unused subscriptions, negotiating better rates, and optimizing memberships.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Scope \- What's Covered**               | \- Identifying all recurring monthly and annual expenses \- Finding and cancelling unused paid services and apps \- Proactively negotiating lower rates on regular bills (internet, cell phone, insurance).- Performing an annual financial health check-up.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Authority \- XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Review financial statements to compile a list of all recurring costs \- Propose a list of subscriptions for cancellation based on pre-defined rules. \- Call providers to negotiate better rates (with prior authorization).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| **Exceptions \- Must Confirm**            | \- The final list of which specific subscriptions to cancel. \- Any negotiation outcome that significantly changes service terms.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Information & Tools Provided**          | \- Secure, read-only access to 1-2 months of financial statements. \- Client's rules for cancellations (e.g., "cancel if unused for 3 months"). \- A shared spreadsheet for tracking audit results.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Approval Thresholds**                   | N/A                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**   | \- XP sends the "Subscription Audit Report" for client review and approval. \- XP sends the "Final Savings Summary" upon completion of the audit.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **SOP \- Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Review Statements:** Securely review financial statements and list all recurring charges in a tracker. 2\. **Propose Cancellations:** Present a "Subscription Audit Report," flagging unused services for cancellation. 3\. **Execute Changes:** After client approval, cancel subscriptions and negotiate with providers for better rates. 4\. **Optimize:** Research and apply any available discounts from existing memberships. 5\. **Report Savings:** Deliver the "Final Savings Summary," detailing all actions taken and the total amount saved. |
| **Final Result**                          | The client's recurring expenses are minimized, and their finances are decluttered without them spending hours on the phone with providers. They save real money and gain peace of mind knowing they are only paying for what they truly use.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Agreement**                             | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |

#### Worked Sample

Following the quarterly audit, the XP sent the client the final summary report:

- **Actions Taken**:
    - Cancelled 3 unused subscriptions (MasterClass, The Athletic, an old SaaS tool).
    - Negotiated a 20% discount on the Comcast internet bill.
- **Total Savings**: **$75/month** (which is **$900/year**).

### Subscription Detox Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                     |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Subscription Detox                                                                                                                          |
| **Purpose**                              | Remove unnecessary recurring costs and optimize active subscriptions.                                                                       |

| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Identify \+ cancel subscriptions under $50/month if unused 60+ days.                                                                     |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Canceling subscriptions over $50/month. \- Business-critical services.                                                                   |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Subscription logins. \- Expense tracker.                                                                                                 |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- \<$50/month unused ‚Üí XP cancels. \- $50‚Äì$200/month ‚Üí notify. \- \>$200/month ‚Üí explicit approval.                                        |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Quarterly subscription report.                                                                                                           |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. Pull active subscriptions list. 2\. Flag unused/duplicates. 3\. Cancel per thresholds. 4\. Update tracker. 5\. Share quarterly savings. |
| **Final Result**                         | Client saves $1,000s/year with no subscription creep.                                                                                       |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                    |

#### Worked Sample **‚Äì Q1 Detox**

- Cancelled ‚Üí $372/year saved.

- Report: ‚Äú‚úÖ Cancelled 2 subs, $372 annual savings. Current active subs: 18.‚Äù

| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- List of subscriptions. \- Secure payment info.                                                                                                                                   |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Discounts/switches within same provider ‚Üí proceed. \- New vendors or contracts ‚Üí explicit approval.                                                                              |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Bi-annual ‚ÄúDiscount Report‚Äù with savings logged.                                                                                                                                 |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. Every 6 months, XP reviews all plans. 2\. Call providers to request discounts. 3\. Apply new promo codes/rates. 4\. Document savings in tracker. 5\. Deliver ‚ÄúDiscount Report.‚Äù |
| **Final Result**                         | Client consistently pays the lowest available rates without effort.                                                                                                                 |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                            |

- NYT Digital: switched to promo rate $5/mo ($96/year saved).

- Total Savings: $408/year.

### Give First Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Give First Protocol                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| **Purpose**                              | Strengthen relationships by consistently offering value first‚Äîthrough introductions, resources, or opportunities‚Äîso the client becomes known as a generous connector.                                                                                                                                         |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Warm introductions. \- Sharing resources (articles, podcasts, tools). \- Passing along relevant opportunities (speaking, jobs, investments).                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Identify 3‚Äì5 ‚Äúgive first‚Äù opportunities weekly. \- Draft intro/resource notes in client‚Äôs tone.                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Intros involving board members, investors, or highly sensitive relationships. \- Opportunities with potential conflicts.                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Client‚Äôs personal CRM (Clay/LinkedIn). \- Content feeds (HBR, McKinsey, industry newsletters). \- Client‚Äôs resource preferences (articles, books, podcasts).                                                                                                                                               |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Routine intros/resources ‚Üí proceed with client review. \- VIP-level introductions ‚Üí explicit client approval.                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Weekly ‚ÄúGive First‚Äù briefing via Slack/Notion (list of suggested intros/resources).                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **Weekly** ‚Üí XP reviews CRM \+ news feeds. 2\. Identify 3‚Äì5 opportunities to add value (intro, resource, invite). 3\. Draft notes in client‚Äôs voice. 4\. Share ‚ÄúGive First‚Äù briefing with client. 5\. Client approves/edits in \<10 minutes. 6\. XP sends/schedules approved outreach \+ logs in tracker. |
| **Final Result**                         | Client consistently adds value in their network ‚Üí reputation as a trusted connector compounds.                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Give First Protocol                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |

#### Worked Example

March 7 ‚ÄúGive First‚Äù Briefing

- **Intro Opportunity:**
    - _Alex Chen_ (early-stage founder) ‚Üí _Priya S._ (angel investor).
    - Draft note: ‚ÄúPriya, meet Alex‚Äîbuilding in AI healthcare. Alex, Priya‚Äôs been supporting founders in your space for years.‚Äù

- **Resource Share:**
    - _To Jordan L._ (CMO contact).
      Draft note: ‚ÄúSaw this McKinsey piece on Gen Z marketing‚Äîthought of you. Curious how it aligns with what you‚Äôre seeing.‚Äù

- **Opportunity Share:**
    - _To Samantha R._ (friend exploring speaking).
    - Draft note: ‚ÄúSpotted this panel on women in tech leadership. Would you like me to nominate you?‚Äù

**Execution:** Client approves in 8 minutes. XP sends messages \+ logs them.
**Result:** 3 touchpoints ‚Üí client strengthens ties across investors, peers, and friends with zero admin load.

---

# Family Time

### Date Night Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Date Night Protocol                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Purpose**                              | Ensure consistent quality time with partner through effortless, well-planned date nights/lunches/activities.                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- At least 1 date night or day activity monthly. \- XP handles all logistics: reservations, childcare, payments, reminders.                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Book activities/restaurants up to $300. \- Arrange childcare from pre-approved list. \- Track what works/what doesn‚Äôt for future planning.                                                                                                                                                                           |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Activities \>$300. \- Any new childcare provider not on approved list.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Shared calendar access. \- List of childcare providers. \- Payment card in 1Password.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Up to $300 ‚Üí XP proceeds. \- $300‚Äì$600 ‚Üí Notify client. \- \>$600 ‚Üí Explicit approval.                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Monthly proposal of 2‚Äì3 options. \- Confirmed event added to shared calendar \+ Slack reminder 3 days prior.                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **T-4 Weeks** ‚Üí XP proposes 2‚Äì3 activities with budget \+ logistics. 2\. **T-3 Weeks** ‚Üí Client confirms choice. 3\. **T-2 Weeks** ‚Üí XP books venue/activity \+ childcare. 4\. **T-3 Days** ‚Üí XP sends Slack reminder with itinerary. 5\. **Post-Date** ‚Üí XP logs ‚Äúworks/doesn‚Äôt work‚Äù notes in Date Night Tracker. |
| **Final Result**                         | Partner feels prioritized, client enjoys stress-free quality time.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

#### Worked Example

March Date Night

- **Options Proposed:** Italian dinner at Via Matta, cooking class, or jazz show.
- **Client Picked:** Jazz show.
- **Logistics:** XP booked tickets ($220), reserved pre-show dinner ($120), booked babysitter (8‚Äì11pm).
- **Execution:** Slack reminder 3 days prior: ‚Äúüé∂ Jazz night this Sat\! Dinner 6:30pm, show 8pm, sitter confirmed.‚Äù
- **Result:** Client \+ partner enjoyed seamless evening. XP logged ‚Äúlive music \= great, late nights less ideal.‚Äù

---

### Weekend Wonder Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| ---------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Weekend Wonder Protocol                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Purpose**                              | Design one ‚Äúperfect day‚Äù each week for family joy, novelty, and connection.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Saturday or Sunday. \- 100% planned: events, meals, travel time. \- Local/tourist-in-your-own-city activities.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Propose and book local activities within 60-minute drive. \- Reserve restaurants and tickets up to $400 total.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Day trips requiring flights/hotels. \- Activities \>$400.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Client‚Äôs family preferences \+ dietary restrictions. \- Budget \+ distance threshold.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Up to $400 ‚Üí proceed. \- $400‚Äì$800 ‚Üí Notify client. \- \>$800 ‚Üí Explicit approval.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Weekly plan sent every Wednesday. \- Full itinerary (minute-by-minute) in shared calendar \+ Slack.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **T-1 Week (Wed)** ‚Üí XP checks local events, drafts 2 itinerary options. 2\. **T-5 Days (Fri)** ‚Üí Client confirms choice. 3\. **T-3 Days** ‚Üí XP books meals, tickets, travel. 4\. **Day-Of** ‚Üí XP sends 9am Slack note: ‚ÄúüìÖ Your Weekend Wonder: see calendar for full plan.‚Äù 5\. **Post** ‚Üí Log feedback: what family enjoyed, what to adjust. |
| **Final Result**                         | Family enjoys novel, curated experiences weekly ‚Üí more joy, less planning burden.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |

#### Worked Example

**April Weekend Wonder**

- **Theme:** Tourist in your own city.
- **Plan:**
    - 9:00am ‚Üí Breakfast at home (XP pre-ordered bakery box).
    - 10:30am ‚Üí Visit new science museum exhibit (tickets booked).
    - 12:30pm ‚Üí Picnic in park (XP arranged pre-packed basket).
    - 2:00pm ‚Üí Family bike ride (XP rented bikes nearby).
    - 6:00pm ‚Üí Dinner at casual family spot (reservation confirmed).

- **Execution:** XP calendarized every block, including travel. Slack message: ‚Äú‚úÖ Family Wonder Day ready‚Äîsee calendar for details.‚Äù
  **Result:** Family loved picnic \+ bikes, feedback logged: ‚Äúkeep outdoor focus, kids enjoyed hands-on exhibits.‚Äù

---

### Milestone Memories Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| ---------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Milestone Memories                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Purpose**                              | Ensure every family/relationship milestone is celebrated thoughtfully, without client managing details.                                                                                                                                                                            |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Anniversaries, birthdays, graduations, promotions. \- Surprise gestures (flowers, notes, framed photos).                                                                                                                                                                        |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Order gifts, flowers, cards up to $300. \- Book reservations at favorite venues. \- Arrange delivery (cake, photos, keepsakes).                                                                                                                                                 |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Any spend \>$300. \- Travel-related celebrations.                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Family calendar of milestones. \- Approved vendor list (florists, gift sites, restaurants).                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Up to $300 ‚Üí proceed. \- $300‚Äì$750 ‚Üí notify. \- \>$750 ‚Üí explicit approval.                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Monthly ‚ÄúMilestone Report‚Äù listing upcoming events.                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **T-1 Month** ‚Üí XP reviews upcoming milestones. 2\. Draft plan: gift, reservation, or gesture. 3\. Confirm budget if \>$300. 4\. **T-2 Weeks** ‚Üí Execute orders/bookings. 5\. **Day-Of** ‚Üí Send Slack reminder with details. 6\. **Post** ‚Üí Log what worked/didn‚Äôt in tracker. |
| **Final Result**                         | Partner/kids never feel forgotten; milestones marked with thoughtful touches.                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |

#### Worked Example

**Anniversary**

- **Event:** 12th wedding anniversary, June 14\.
- **Plan:** XP booked favorite Italian restaurant ($180), ordered bouquet delivery ($95), arranged childcare ($120).
- **Execution:** Slack reminder morning of: ‚Äúüíê Dinner 7pm tonight, flowers delivered at 5pm, sitter arrives 6:30pm.‚Äù
- **Result:** Partner delighted, client stress-free; XP logged ‚Äúromantic dinners always a hit.‚Äù

---

### Family Traditions Protocol

| Section                                  | Details                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **Protocol Title**                       | Family Traditions                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| **Purpose**                              | Build recurring family rituals (weekly, monthly, or quarterly) that create connection and joy.                                                                                                                                             |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**               | \- Weekly/monthly Sunday dinners. \- Family activities (cooking, crafts, outings). \- Seasonal/holiday rituals.                                                                                                                            |
| **Authority ‚Äì XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Choose recipes/activities from trusted sources (NYT Cooking, FT recipes, Ottolenghi, etc.). \- Order groceries/supplies in advance. \- Propose 2‚Äì3 activity ideas (indoor, outdoor, creative).                                          |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì Must Confirm**            | \- Activities requiring \>$200 spend. \- Any unusual/out-of-scope events (overnight trips, travel).                                                                                                                                        |
| **Information & Tools Provided**         | \- Family preferences (cuisine, activities, allergies). \- Approved budget \+ vendors.                                                                                                                                                     |
| **Approval Thresholds**                  | \- Up to $200 ‚Üí proceed. \- $200‚Äì$500 ‚Üí notify. \- \>$500 ‚Üí explicit approval.                                                                                                                                                             |
| **Preferred Communication & Frequency**  | \- Monthly proposal of tradition ideas via Slack.                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| **SOP ‚Äì Step by Step**                   | 1\. **T-2 Weeks** ‚Üí XP proposes 2‚Äì3 options (cooking, craft, outing). 2\. Client picks or XP defaults. 3\. **T-1 Week** ‚Üí Order groceries/supplies. 4\. **Day-Of** ‚Üí Send Slack reminder \+ itinerary. 5\. **Post** ‚Üí Log family feedback. |
| **Final Result**                         | Family builds meaningful rituals‚Äîcooking together, exploring, or creating‚Äîwithout client planning burden.                                                                                                                                  |
| **Agreement**                            | Client: \_\_\_\_\_\_ XP: \_\_\_\_\_\_ Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_                                                                                                                                                                                   |

#### Worked Example

**Monthly Family Tradition (March)**

- **Theme:** Sunday Dinner \+ Activity.
- **Plan:** XP proposed 3 options:
    1. NYT Cooking recipe (sheet-pan paella).
    2. Pottery painting at local studio.
    3. Indoor rock climbing session.
       **Client Chose:** Pottery painting.
- **Execution:** XP booked 2-hour pottery class ($160), ordered light dinner (pasta \+ salad kit, $60).
- **Reminder:** Slack AM message: ‚Äúüé® Pottery 2‚Äì4pm today, dinner kit in fridge for 6pm.‚Äù
- **Result:** Family loved activity ‚Üí XP logged feedback: ‚ÄúHands-on activities \= big hit.‚Äù

# Delegation Curriculum

**Delegation Foundations**

- How to delegate
    - Delete Annoyance (simple relief)
        - Never wait on hold again
        - Never shop online again
        - Never RSVP again
        - Never read/pay for subscriptions you don‚Äôt want

    - Own Your Day (intentional design)
        - Inbox predrafts
        - Calendar reset
        - Exercise lock
        - Goal guard

    - Run Life Like a Hotel (systemized living)
        - Stock refill
        - Remote home manager
        - Personal concierge desk

    - Multiply Your Impact (scale without strain)
        - Build influence
            - Salon diners
            - Great gifts
            - Relationship tracker
            - Capital commitments
        - Hiring Engine
            - Talent magnet
        - Get smarter
            - Book-to-action
            - Custom podcasts
            - News brief
            - Peer circles
        - Be a better boss
            - First day recognition
            - Team recognition

    - Live the Next Version of You (Black Diamond Delegation)
        - Energy, Health, Wellness
            - Nutrition concierge
            - Energy calendar
            - Bedtime ritual
            - Sleep score scheduling
            - Jet lag reset
            - Remote alarm
            - Decision filter
        - Family and Home
            - Homework buddy
            - Family historian
            - Personal CRM
            - Quick touchpoints
            - Relationship builder
            - Date nights
            - Weekend wonders
            - Milestone memories
            - Family traditions

- Methods of delegation
    - Thumbs (Emergency Only)
    - Fingers (Standard)
    - Voice (Speed Champion)
    - Proactive Delegation (Ultimate Leverage)

- Protocols and SOPs
    - Travel Management
    - Inbox Management
    - Calendar Management
    - Payments & Purchases
    - Expense Reports
    - Event Management
    - Health & Wellness
    - Home & Personal Admin
    - Project Management
    - Document & File Management
    - Communication & Social Media
    - Research & Briefing

- Cardinal Sins of Delegation

**Delegation Mastery**

- How to build trust
    - Method: The Horse Race
    - Method: Weekly Activities Report (WAR)

- How to delegate clearly
    - Method: Four Pillars

- How to build a delegation system
    - Method: Commitment Moments
    - Method: Feedback Loops
    - Method: Work Environment Audit
    - Template: Weekly Exec-XP System Alignment

- How to balance autonomy and control
    - Method: Trust and Teach
    - Method: Command and Control

- How to measure and improve delegation
    - Method: 3 Tests
    - Template: Decision Guide

- How to create a safe space to learn
    - Framework: Low threat, high challenge
    - Method: Focus on the future

# Judgement and Execution Library

# **üìò Athena Delegation Playbook**

### **Protocols & SOPs for Seamless Executive Partnership**

---

## **Cover Page**

**Prepared for:** \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_
**Member Name**

**Prepared by:** \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_
**Executive Partner (XP)**

**Date:** \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**Version:** 1.0

---

## **Quick-Start Guide**

### **üéØ Purpose of This Playbook**

This Delegation Playbook defines the rules, boundaries, and workflows that make executive delegation effortless. Each protocol sets what success looks like, what‚Äôs off-limits, and how your XP executes independently ‚Äî so you stay focused on high-impact leadership.

### **üõ† How to Use**

1. **Choose a Domain** ‚Üí Travel, Inbox, Calendar, Payments, Projects, etc.
2. **Fill the Template Together** ‚Üí Client provides preferences \+ rules; XP captures details.
3. **Sign Off** ‚Üí Both confirm agreement at the bottom.
4. **Store in Shared Folder** ‚Üí All protocols live in one Playbook file.
5. **Review Quarterly** ‚Üí Update thresholds, tools, or preferences as needs evolve.

### **‚úÖ Why It Works**

- **Clarity** ‚Üí No ambiguity about authority, exceptions, or tools.
- **Consistency** ‚Üí Every task follows the same SOP structure.
- **Control** ‚Üí Approval thresholds \+ reporting rules keep you in charge without micromanaging.
- **Confidence** ‚Üí Client and XP work from the same playbook, aligned and accountable.

## **üìä Protocol Index ‚Äì At a Glance**

| Domain   | Icon | Scope                      | XP Authority                    | Exceptions               | Updates                            |
| -------- | ---- | -------------------------- | ------------------------------- | ------------------------ | ---------------------------------- |
| Travel   | ‚úàÔ∏è   | Flights, hotels, transport | Book prefs, rebook \< $500      | Intl trips, \> $2,500    | Slack \+ calendar notes            |
| Inbox    | üìß   | Triage, drafting           | Archive, draft replies          | Board/legal/finance      | Daily digest \+ Slack ping         |
| Calendar | üìÖ   | Scheduling, blocking       | Decline low-priority            | Board/travel             | Daily snapshot \+ weekly lookahead |
| Payments | üí≥   | Purchases, bills           | Orders \< $250, recurring bills | \> $250, new vendors     | Real-time \+ weekly summary        |
| Expenses | üßæ   | Reports, reconciliation    | Submit \< $5,000                | \> $5,000 unusual        | Weekly \+ monthly summary          |
| Events   | üçΩÔ∏è   | Dinners, offsites          | Book venues \< $5,000           | Speakers/guests          | Slack \+ weekly check-in           |
| Health   | üè•   | Appointments, checkups     | Book recurring providers        | New specialists, \> $500 | Monthly summary                    |
| Home     | üè°   | Utilities, vendors         | Pay bills, vendors \< $500      | New vendors, \> $500     | Real-time updates                  |
| Projects | üìÇ   | Task tracking              | Manage tracker                  | Scope changes            | Weekly digest                      |
| Docs     | üìë   | Filing, versioning         | Organize, naming rules          | Legal/board docs         | Monthly summary                    |
| Social   | üì£   | Posts, monitoring          | Draft/schedule posts            | Sensitive/controversial  | Weekly plan                        |
| Research | üîç   | Briefings, scans           | Compile \+ summarize            | Due diligence            | Per request                        |

## **Worked Examples**

## **1\. Travel Management**

| Section                                       | Details to Complete                                                                       |
| --------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**                            | Travel Management                                                                         |
| **Purpose**                                   | Defines rules and boundaries for delegating all travel booking.                           |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered**                    | \- Flights \- Hotels \- Ground transport \- Visa documentation                            |
| **Authority ‚Äì What XP Can Do Without Asking** | \- Book within approved preferences \- Apply loyalty numbers \- Rebook flights under $500 |
| **Exceptions ‚Äì When XP Must Confirm**         | \- International trips \- Costs \>$2,500 \- New vendors                                   |
| **Information & Tools Provided**              | \- Loyalty logins in 1Password \- Corporate card \- Travel profile                        |
| **Approval Thresholds**                       | Up to $2,500 ‚Üí proceed $2,500‚Äì$5,000 ‚Üí notify Above $5,000 ‚Üí explicit approval            |
| **Updates**                                   | Slack \+ calendar notes Real-time for bookings, weekly digest                             |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**                               | Receive request ‚Üí Confirm details ‚Üí Book ‚Üí Share itinerary/receipt ‚Üí Add to calendar      |
| **Final Result**                              | Complete itineraries with receipts \+ loyalty points applied.                             |

## **2\. Inbox Management**

| Section                    | Details to Complete                                            |
| -------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**         | Inbox Management                                               |
| **Purpose**                | Reduce inbox clutter; delegate triage and drafting.            |
| **Scope ‚Äì What‚Äôs Covered** | \- Filtering \- Flagging urgent items \- Drafting responses    |
| **Authority**              | \- Archive/delete low-value emails \- Draft standard responses |
| **Exceptions**             | \- Board/legal/financial correspondence                        |
| **Information & Tools**    | \- Gmail delegated access \- Style guide                       |
| **Updates**                | Daily digest email; Slack ping for urgent                      |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**            | Review ‚Üí Tag/triage ‚Üí Draft ‚Üí Notify client ‚Üí Track follow-ups |
| **Final Result**           | Inbox zero; only high-value items reach client.                |

## **3\. Calendar Management**

| Section            | Details to Complete                                                              |
| ------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title** | Calendar Management                                                              |
| **Purpose**        | Protect client‚Äôs time and priorities.                                            |
| **Scope**          | \- Scheduling \- Time blocking \- Meeting prep                                   |
| **Authority**      | \- Decline low-priority meetings \- Accept per rules \- Adjust blocks            |
| **Exceptions**     | \- Board-level \- Travel-related                                                 |
| **Tools**          | Google Calendar; preference doc                                                  |
| **Updates**        | Slack daily snapshot; weekly email lookahead                                     |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**    | Review requests ‚Üí Apply rules ‚Üí Confirm/decline ‚Üí Add prep notes ‚Üí Share updates |
| **Final Result**   | Aligned calendar with focus preserved.                                           |

## **4\. Payments & Purchases**

| Section                 | Example                                                                                                                 |
| ----------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title**      | Payments & Purchases                                                                                                    |
| **Scope**               | Online shopping, bills, subscriptions                                                                                   |
| **Authority**           | Use 1Password, orders \< $250, recurring bills                                                                          |
| **Exceptions**          | Purchases \> $250, new vendors, unapproved addresses                                                                    |
| **Approval Thresholds** | Up to $250 ‚Üí proceed $250‚Äì$1,000 ‚Üí notify Above $1,000 ‚Üí explicit approval                                              |
| **Updates**             | Slack; real-time if \>$250, weekly summary otherwise                                                                    |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**         | 1\. Client sends link 2\. XP confirms details 3\. Execute purchase 4\. Slack update \+ save receipt 5\. Verify delivery |
| **Final Result**        | Client never enters card details; XP completes purchase securely with receipts stored.                                  |
| **Agreement**           | Client Signature: Alex Smith XP Signature: Jordan Lee Date: Sept 3, 2025                                                |

## **5\. Expense Reports**

| Section            | Example                                                 |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title** | Expense Reports                                         |
| **Scope**          | \- Credit card reconciliation \- Monthly expense filing |
| **Authority**      | Submit reports under $5,000                             |
| **Exceptions**     | Unusual vendors or \>$5,000                             |
| **Tools**          | Expensify, Amex, receipts folder                        |
| **Updates**        | Weekly Slack \+ monthly summary                         |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**    | Collect receipts ‚Üí Categorize ‚Üí Submit ‚Üí Save PDF copy  |
| **Final Result**   | Reports filed on time, zero client effort.              |

| ------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------- |

| **Exceptions**     | New specialists or costs \>$500                                  |

## **8\. Home & Personal Admin**

| Section            | Example                                                 |
| ------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title** | Home & Personal Admin                                   |
| **Scope**          | \- Utilities \- Household vendors \- Deliveries         |
| **Authority**      | Pay utilities Schedule vendors under $500               |
| **Exceptions**     | New vendors or \>$500                                   |
| **Tools**          | 1Password, shared sheet                                 |
| **Updates**        | Slack real-time                                         |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**    | Receive request ‚Üí Book vendor/pay bill ‚Üí Confirm update |
| **Final Result**   | Home runs smoothly, no admin burden.                    |

## **9\. Project Management**

| Section            | Example                                               |
| ------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------- |
| **Protocol Title** | Project Management                                    |
| **Scope**          | \- Task tracking \- Deadlines \- Team coordination    |
| **Authority**      | Update tracker; follow up with collaborators          |
| **Exceptions**     | Strategic scope changes                               |
| **Tools**          | Asana/Notion                                          |
| **Updates**        | Weekly digest                                         |
| **SOP ‚Äì Steps**    | Log tasks ‚Üí Clarify ‚Üí Track ‚Üí Report status           |
| **Final Result**   | Projects move forward without client chasing details. |
